I've uploaded a code repository in the directory . Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Footer detection absorbs body text on pages with nearby notes
## Context
Parent issue: #354 — reported by @jsmount on v2.0.2 with CERAGEM BALANCE user manual (52 pages).

## Problem
Footer detection over-extends on pages where body text is spatially close to the footer region.

**Pages 19–20:** Footer bounding box extends to y=135 (h≈100) instead of the normal y=43 (h≈9). This absorbs the body note `※ 출수 중 출수 버튼을 터치하면 출수가 정지됩니다.` (at y=116) into the footer element.

**Page 21:** Same document, same footer pattern — footer is correctly detected with compact bbox (h=9.2).

**Pages 6, 20:** Footer text (`06 CERAGEM BALANCE USER MANUAL`, `20 CERAGEM BALANCE USER MANUAL`) leaks into Markdown output instead of being filtered.

## Data

| Page | Footer bbox height | Body text absorbed? | Footer text in MD? |
|------|--------------------|--------------------|--------------------|
| 18   | 9.2                | No                 | No                 |
| 19   | 100.4              | Yes (※ note)       | No                 |
| 20   | 100.4              | Yes (※ note)       | Yes                |
| 21   | 9.2                | No                 | No                 |

## Reproduction
```bash
pip install opendataloader-pdf==2.0.2
# PDF: CERAGEM_BALANCE_사용설명서.pdf (in odl-test-fixtures/inbox/354-text-ordering-footer-detection/)
opendataloader-pdf convert --format json --pages 19,20,21 CERAGEM_BALANCE_사용설명서.pdf
# Check footer bounding box heights in JSON output
```

    39	/**
    40	 * Processor for detecting and extracting headers and footers from PDF documents.
    41	 * Identifies repeating content at the top and bottom of pages.
    42	 */
    43	public class HeaderFooterProcessor {
    44	
    45	    /**
    46	     * Processes document contents to detect headers and footers.
    47	     *
    48	     * @param contents the document contents organized by page
    49	     * @param isTagged whether the document is tagged
    50	     */
    51	    public static void processHeadersAndFooters(List<List<IObject>> contents, boolean isTagged) {
    52	        DocumentProcessor.setIndexesForDocumentContents(contents);
    53	        List<List<IObject>> sortedContents = new ArrayList<>();
    54	        for (List<IObject> content : contents) {
    55	            sortedContents.add(DocumentProcessor.sortPageContents(content));
    56	        }
    57	        List<List<IObject>> filteredSortedContents = new ArrayList<>();
    58	        for (List<IObject> content : sortedContents) {
    59	            filteredSortedContents.add(content.stream().filter(c -> !(c instanceof LineChunk) && !(c instanceof LineArtChunk)).collect(Collectors.toList()));
    60	        }
    61	        List<SemanticHeaderOrFooter> footers = getHeadersOrFooters(filteredSortedContents, false);
    62	        List<SemanticHeaderOrFooter> headers = getHeadersOrFooters(filteredSortedContents, true);
    63	        for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < contents.size(); pageNumber++) {
    64	            contents.set(pageNumber, updatePageContents(contents.get(pageNumber), headers.get(pageNumber), footers.get(pageNumber)));
    65	        }
    66	        if (!isTagged) {
    67	            processHeadersOrFootersContents(footers);
    68	            processHeadersOrFootersContents(headers);
    69	        }
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    private static void processHeadersOrFootersContents(List<SemanticHeaderOrFooter> headersOrFooters) {
    73	        for (SemanticHeaderOrFooter headerOrFooter : headersOrFooters) {
    74	            if (headerOrFooter != null) {
    75	                headerOrFooter.setContents(processHeaderOrFooterContent(headerOrFooter.getContents()));
    76	            }
    77	        }
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    private static List<IObject> updatePageContents(List<IObject> pageContents, SemanticHeaderOrFooter header, SemanticHeaderOrFooter footer) {
    81	        SortedSet<Integer> headerAndFooterIndexes = new TreeSet<>();
    82	        headerAndFooterIndexes.addAll(getHeaderOrFooterContentsIndexes(header));
    83	        headerAndFooterIndexes.addAll(getHeaderOrFooterContentsIndexes(footer));
    84	        if (headerAndFooterIndexes.isEmpty()) {
    85	            return pageContents;
    86	        }
    87	        List<IObject> result = new ArrayList<>();
    88	        if (header != null) {
    89	            result.add(header);
    90	        }
    91	        Iterator<Integer> iterator = headerAndFooterIndexes.iterator();
    92	        int nextHeaderOrFooterIndex = iterator.hasNext() ? iterator.next() : pageContents.size();
    93	        for (int index = 0; index < pageContents.size(); index++) {
    94	            if (index < nextHeaderOrFooterIndex) {
    95	                result.add(pageContents.get(index));
    96	            } else {
    97	                nextHeaderOrFooterIndex = iterator.hasNext() ? iterator.next() : pageContents.size();
    98	            }
    99	        }
   100	        if (footer != null) {
   101	            result.add(footer);
   102	        }
   103	        return result;
   104	    }
   105	
   106	    private static Set<Integer> getHeaderOrFooterContentsIndexes(SemanticHeaderOrFooter header) {
   107	        if (header == null) {
   108	            return Collections.emptySet();
   109	        }
   110	        SortedSet<Integer> set = new TreeSet<>();
   111	        for (IObject content : header.getContents()) {
   112	            set.add(content.getIndex());
   113	        }
   114	        return set;
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    private static List<SemanticHeaderOrFooter> getHeadersOrFooters(List<List<IObject>> sortedContents, boolean isHeaderDetection) {
   118	        List<SemanticHeaderOrFooter> headersOrFooters = new ArrayList<>(sortedContents.size());
   119	        List<Integer> numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage = getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage(sortedContents, isHeaderDetection);
   120	        for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < sortedContents.size(); pageNumber++) {
   121	            Integer currentIndex = numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage.get(pageNumber);
   122	            if (currentIndex == 0) {
   123	                headersOrFooters.add(null);
   124	                continue;
   125	            }
   126	            List<IObject> pageContents = sortedContents.get(pageNumber);
   127	            List<IObject> headerContents = filterHeaderOrFooterContents(isHeaderDetection ? pageContents.subList(0, currentIndex) :
   128	                    pageContents.subList(pageContents.size() - currentIndex, pageContents.size()), pageNumber, isHeaderDetection);
   129	            if (headerContents.isEmpty()) {
   130	                headersOrFooters.add(null);
   131	                continue;
   132	            }
   133	            SemanticHeaderOrFooter semanticHeaderOrFooter = new SemanticHeaderOrFooter(isHeaderDetection ? SemanticType.HEADER : SemanticType.FOOTER);
   134	            semanticHeaderOrFooter.addContents(headerContents);
   135	            semanticHeaderOrFooter.setRecognizedStructureId(StaticLayoutContainers.incrementContentId());
   136	            headersOrFooters.add(semanticHeaderOrFooter);
   137	        }
   138	        return headersOrFooters;
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    private static List<IObject> processHeaderOrFooterContent(List<IObject> contents) {
   142	        List<IObject> newContents = ParagraphProcessor.processParagraphs(contents);
   143	        newContents = ListProcessor.processListsFromTextNodes(newContents);
   144	        HeadingProcessor.processHeadings(newContents, false);
   145	        DocumentProcessor.setIDs(newContents);
   146	        CaptionProcessor.processCaptions(newContents);
   147	        return newContents;
   148	    }
   149	
   150	    private static List<Integer> getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage(List<List<IObject>> sortedContents, boolean isHeaderDetection) {
   151	        List<Integer> numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage = new ArrayList<>(sortedContents.size());
   152	        for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < sortedContents.size(); pageNumber++) {
   153	            numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage.add(0);
   154	        }
   155	        int currentIndex = 0;
   156	        while (true) {
   157	            List<IObject> contents = new ArrayList<>(sortedContents.size());
   158	            for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < sortedContents.size(); pageNumber++) {
   159	                if (numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage.get(pageNumber) != currentIndex) {
   160	                    contents.add(null);
   161	                    continue;
   162	                }
   163	                List<IObject> pageContents = sortedContents.get(pageNumber);
   164	                int index = isHeaderDetection ? currentIndex : pageContents.size() - 1 - currentIndex;
   165	                if (index >= 0 && index < pageContents.size()) {
   166	                    contents.add(pageContents.get(index));
   167	                } else {
   168	                    contents.add(null);
   169	                }
   170	            }
   171	            Set<Integer> newIndexes = getIndexesOfHeaderOrFootersContents(contents);
   172	            if (newIndexes.isEmpty()) {
   173	                break;
   174	            }
   175	            for (Integer newIndex : newIndexes) {
   176	                numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage.set(newIndex, currentIndex + 1);
   177	            }
   178	            currentIndex++;
   179	        }
   180	        return numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage;
   181	    }
   182	
   183	    private static Set<Integer> getIndexesOfHeaderOrFootersContents(List<IObject> contents) {
   184	        Set<Integer> result = new HashSet<>(contents.size());
   185	        for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < contents.size() - 1; pageNumber++) {
   186	            IObject currentObject = contents.get(pageNumber);
   187	            IObject nextObject = contents.get(pageNumber + 1);
   188	            if (currentObject != null && nextObject != null) {
   189	                if (arePossibleHeadersOrFooters(currentObject, nextObject, 1)) {
   190	                    result.add(pageNumber);
   191	                    result.add(pageNumber + 1);
   192	                }
   193	            }
   194	        }
   195	        //2-page style
   196	        for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < contents.size() - 2; pageNumber++) {
   197	            IObject currentObject = contents.get(pageNumber);
   198	            IObject nextObject = contents.get(pageNumber + 2);
   199	            if (currentObject != null && nextObject != null) {
   200	                if (arePossibleHeadersOrFooters(currentObject, nextObject, 2)) {
   201	                    result.add(pageNumber);
   202	                    result.add(pageNumber + 2);
   203	                }
   204	            }
   205	        }
   206	        return result;
   207	    }
   208	
   209	    /**
   210	     * Checks if a content object is a header or footer.
   211	     *
   212	     * @param content the content object to check
   213	     * @return true if the content is a header or footer, false otherwise
   214	     */
   215	    public static boolean isHeaderOrFooter(IObject content) {
   216	        if (content instanceof INode) {
   217	            INode node = (INode) content;
   218	            if (node.getSemanticType() == SemanticType.HEADER || node.getSemanticType() == SemanticType.FOOTER) {
   219	                return true;
   220	            }
   221	        }
   222	        return false;
   223	    }
   224	
   225	    private static List<IObject> filterHeaderOrFooterContents(List<IObject> contents, int pageNumber, boolean isHeaderDetection) {
   226	        BoundingBox boundingBox = DocumentProcessor.getPageBoundingBox(pageNumber);
   227	        if (boundingBox == null) {
   228	            return contents;
   229	        }
   230	        List<IObject> result = new ArrayList<>();
   231	        for (IObject content : contents) {
   232	            if (isHeaderDetection) {
   233	                if (content.getBottomY() < boundingBox.getHeight() * 2 / 3) {
   234	                    continue;
   235	                }
   236	            } else {
   237	                if (content.getTopY() > boundingBox.getHeight() / 3) {
   238	                    continue;
   239	                }
   240	            }
   241	            result.add(content);
   242	        }
   243	        return result;
   244	    }
   245	
   246	    private static boolean arePossibleHeadersOrFooters(IObject object1, IObject object2, int increment) {
   247	        if (object1 instanceof SemanticTextNode && object2 instanceof SemanticTextNode) {
   248	            SemanticTextNode textNode1 = (SemanticTextNode) object1;
   249	            SemanticTextNode textNode2 = (SemanticTextNode) object2;
   250	            if (!BoundingBox.areOverlapsBoundingBoxesExcludingPages(object1.getBoundingBox(), object2.getBoundingBox())) {
   251	                return false;
   252	            }
   253	            if (!NodeUtils.areCloseNumbers(textNode1.getFontSize(), textNode2.getFontSize())) {
   254	                return false;
   255	            }
   256	            if (Objects.equals(textNode1.getValue(), textNode2.getValue())) {
   257	                return true;
   258	            }
   259	            List<SemanticTextNode> textNodes = new ArrayList<>(2);
   260	            textNodes.add(textNode1);
   261	            textNodes.add(textNode2);
   262	            if (getHeadersOrFootersIntervals(textNodes, increment).size() == 1) {
   263	                return true;
   264	            }
   265	        } else if (object1 instanceof TextLine && object2 instanceof TextLine) {
   266	            TextLine line1 = (TextLine) object1;
   267	            TextLine line2 = (TextLine) object2;
   268	            SemanticTextNode textNode1 = new SemanticTextNode();
   269	            textNode1.add(line1);
   270	            SemanticTextNode textNode2 = new SemanticTextNode();
   271	            textNode2.add(line2);
   272	            return arePossibleHeadersOrFooters(textNode1, textNode2, increment);
   273	        } else {
   274	            if (BoundingBox.areSameBoundingBoxesExcludingPages(object1.getBoundingBox(), object2.getBoundingBox())) {
   275	                return true;
   276	            }
   277	        }
   278	        return false;
   279	    }
   280	
   281	    private static Set<ListInterval> getHeadersOrFootersIntervals(List<SemanticTextNode> textNodes, int increment) {
   282	        List<ListItemTextInfo> textChildrenInfo = new ArrayList<>(textNodes.size());
   283	        for (int i = 0; i < textNodes.size(); i++) {
   284	            SemanticTextNode textNode = textNodes.get(i);
   285	            TextLine line = textNode.getFirstNonSpaceLine();
   286	            TextLine secondLine = textNode.getNonSpaceLine(1);
   287	            textChildrenInfo.add(new ListItemTextInfo(i, textNode.getSemanticType(),
   288	                    line, line.getValue().trim(), secondLine == null));
   289	        }
   290	        Set<ListInterval> intervals = getHeadersOfFooterIntervals(textChildrenInfo, increment);
   291	        return intervals;
   292	    }
   293	
   294	    private static Set<ListInterval> getHeadersOfFooterIntervals(List<ListItemTextInfo> itemsInfo, int increment) {
   295	        ListIntervalsCollection listIntervals = new ListIntervalsCollection();
   296	        listIntervals.putAll((new AlfaLettersListLabelsDetectionAlgorithm1(increment)).getItemsIntervals(itemsInfo));
   297	        listIntervals.putAll((new AlfaLettersListLabelsDetectionAlgorithm2(increment)).getItemsIntervals(itemsInfo));
   298	        listIntervals.putAll((new KoreanLettersListLabelsDetectionAlgorithm(increment)).getItemsIntervals(itemsInfo));
   299	        listIntervals.putAll((new RomanNumbersListLabelsDetectionAlgorithm(increment)).getItemsIntervals(itemsInfo));
   300	        ArabicNumbersListLabelsDetectionAlgorithm arabicNumbersListLabelsDetectionAlgorithm = new ArabicNumbersListLabelsDetectionAlgorithm(increment);
   301	        arabicNumbersListLabelsDetectionAlgorithm.setHeaderOrFooterDetection(true);
   302	        listIntervals.putAll((arabicNumbersListLabelsDetectionAlgorithm).getItemsIntervals(itemsInfo));
   303	        ListIntervalsCollection correctIntervals = new ListIntervalsCollection(getEqualsItems(itemsInfo));
   304	        for (ListInterval listInterval : listIntervals.getSet()) {
   305	            List<String> labels = new LinkedList<>();
   306	            for (ListItemInfo info : listInterval.getListItemsInfos()) {
   307	                labels.add(((ListItemTextInfo) info).getListItem());
   308	            }
   309	            if (ListLabelsUtils.isListLabels(labels, increment)) {
   310	                correctIntervals.put(listInterval);
   311	            }
   312	        }
   313	        return correctIntervals.getSet();
   314	    }
   315

   322	                if (interval.getNumberOfListItems() > 1) {

For header detection (`isHeaderDetection=true`):

For footer detection (`isHeaderDetection=false`):

- Then for headers: `pageContents.subList(0, currentIndex)` - first N items

    64	/**
    65	 * Main processor for PDF document analysis and output generation.
    66	 * Coordinates the extraction, processing, and generation of various output formats.
    67	 */
    68	public class DocumentProcessor {
    69	    private static final Logger LOGGER = Logger.getLogger(DocumentProcessor.class.getCanonicalName());
    70	
    71	    /**
    72	     * Processes a PDF file and generates the configured outputs.
    73	     *
    74	     * @param inputPdfName the path to the input PDF file
    75	     * @param config the configuration settings
    76	     * @throws IOException if unable to process the file
    77	     */
    78	    public static void processFile(String inputPdfName, Config config) throws IOException {
    79	        preprocessing(inputPdfName, config);
    80	        calculateDocumentInfo();
    81	        Set<Integer> pagesToProcess = getValidPageNumbers(config);
    82	        List<List<IObject>> contents;
    83	        if (StaticLayoutContainers.isUseStructTree()) {
    84	            contents = TaggedDocumentProcessor.processDocument(inputPdfName, config, pagesToProcess);
    85	        } else if (config.isHybridEnabled()) {
    86	            contents = HybridDocumentProcessor.processDocument(inputPdfName, config, pagesToProcess);
    87	        } else {
    88	            contents = processDocument(inputPdfName, config, pagesToProcess);
    89	        }
    90	        if (config.needsStructuredProcessing()) {
    91	            sortContents(contents, config);
    92	        }
    93	        ContentSanitizer contentSanitizer = new ContentSanitizer(config.getFilterConfig().getFilterRules(),
    94	            config.getFilterConfig().isFilterSensitiveData());
    95	        contentSanitizer.sanitizeContents(contents);
    96	        generateOutputs(inputPdfName, contents, config);
    97	    }
    98	
    99	    /**
   100	     * Validates and filters page numbers from config against actual document pages.
   101	     * Logs warnings for pages that don't exist in the document.
   102	     *
   103	     * @param config the configuration containing page selection
   104	     * @return Set of valid 0-indexed page numbers to process, or null for all pages
   105	     */
   106	    private static Set<Integer> getValidPageNumbers(Config config) {
   107	        List<Integer> requestedPages = config.getPageNumbers();
   108	        if (requestedPages.isEmpty()) {
   109	            return null; // null means process all pages
   110	        }
   111	
   112	        int totalPages = StaticContainers.getDocument().getNumberOfPages();
   113	        Set<Integer> validPages = new LinkedHashSet<>();
   114	        List<Integer> invalidPages = new ArrayList<>();
   115	
   116	        for (Integer page : requestedPages) {
   117	            int zeroIndexed = page - 1; // Convert 1-based to 0-based
   118	            if (zeroIndexed >= 0 && zeroIndexed < totalPages) {
   119	                validPages.add(zeroIndexed);
   120	            } else {
   121	                invalidPages.add(page);
   122	            }
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        if (!invalidPages.isEmpty()) {
   126	            LOGGER.log(Level.WARNING,
   127	                "Requested pages {0} do not exist in document (total pages: {1}). Processing only existing pages: {2}",
   128	                new Object[]{invalidPages, totalPages,
   129	                    validPages.stream().map(p -> p + 1).collect(Collectors.toList())});
   130	        }
   131	
   132	        if (validPages.isEmpty()) {
   133	            LOGGER.log(Level.WARNING,
   134	                "No valid pages to process. Document has {0} pages but requested: {1}",
   135	                new Object[]{totalPages, requestedPages});
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        return validPages;
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   142	    private static List<List<IObject>> processDocument(String inputPdfName, Config config, Set<Integer> pagesToProcess) throws IOException {
   143	        int totalPages = StaticContainers.getDocument().getNumberOfPages();
   144	        List<List<IObject>> contents = new ArrayList<>(Collections.nCopies(totalPages, null));
   145	
   146	        // Capture ALL ThreadLocal state from main thread for propagation to workers
   147	        final var document = StaticContainers.getDocument();
   148	        final var tableBordersCollection = StaticContainers.getTableBordersCollection();
   149	        final var accumulatedNodeMapper = StaticContainers.getAccumulatedNodeMapper();
   150	        final var objectKeyMapper = StaticContainers.getObjectKeyMapper();
   151	        final boolean keepLineBreaks = StaticContainers.isKeepLineBreaks();
   152	        final boolean isDataLoader = StaticContainers.isDataLoader();
   153	        final var isIgnoreCharsWithoutUnicode = StaticContainers.getIsIgnoreCharactersWithoutUnicode();
   154	
   155	        // Capture StaticLayoutContainers state (shared mutable — synchronized list for headings)
   156	        final var headings = StaticLayoutContainers.getHeadings();
   157	        final long contentId = StaticLayoutContainers.getCurrentContentId();
   158	        final boolean useStructTree = StaticLayoutContainers.isUseStructTree();
   159	
   160	        // Runnable that propagates ThreadLocal state to the current (worker) thread
   161	        final Runnable propagateState = () -> {
   162	            // veraPDF StaticContainers
   163	            StaticContainers.setDocument(document);
   164	            StaticContainers.setTableBordersCollection(tableBordersCollection);
   165	            StaticContainers.setAccumulatedNodeMapper(accumulatedNodeMapper);
   166	            StaticContainers.setObjectKeyMapper(objectKeyMapper);
   167	            StaticContainers.setKeepLineBreaks(keepLineBreaks);
   168	            StaticContainers.setIsDataLoader(isDataLoader);
   169	            StaticContainers.setIsIgnoreCharactersWithoutUnicode(isIgnoreCharsWithoutUnicode);
   170	            // Project StaticLayoutContainers — share the same headings list across workers
   171	            StaticLayoutContainers.setHeadings(headings);
   172	            StaticLayoutContainers.setCurrentContentId(contentId);
   173	            StaticLayoutContainers.setIsUseStructTree(useStructTree);
   174	        };
   175	
   176	        // Pre-fetch all page artifacts on main thread (document access is ThreadLocal)
   177	        List<?>[] pageArtifacts = new List<?>[totalPages];
   178	        for (int i = 0; i < totalPages; i++) {
   179	            pageArtifacts[i] = document.getArtifacts(i);
   180	        }
   181	
   182	        int parallelism = Runtime.getRuntime().availableProcessors();
   183	        ForkJoinPool pool = new ForkJoinPool(parallelism);
   184	        LOGGER.log(Level.INFO, "Processing {0} pages with {1} threads", new Object[]{totalPages, parallelism});
   185	
   186	        try {
   187	            // Loop 1: ContentFilter per-page (largest bottleneck)
   188	            pool.submit(() ->
   189	                IntStream.range(0, totalPages).parallel().forEach(pageNumber -> {
   190	                    try {
   191	                        propagateState.run();
   192	                        if (shouldProcessPage(pageNumber, pagesToProcess)) {
   193	                            List<IObject> pageContents = ContentFilterProcessor.getFilteredContents(inputPdfName,
   194	                                (List) pageArtifacts[pageNumber], pageNumber, config);
   195	                            contents.set(pageNumber, pageContents);
   196	                        } else {
   197	                            contents.set(pageNumber, new ArrayList<>());
   198	                        }
   199	                    } catch (IOException e) {
   200	                        throw new UncheckedIOException(e);
   201	                    }
   202	                })
   203	            ).get();
   204	
   205	            // Hidden text detection: sequential post-processing (requires ContrastRatioConsumer
   206	            // which renders PDF pages — not safe to parallelize due to per-thread PDF file I/O)
   207	            if (config.getFilterConfig().isFilterHiddenText()) {
   208	                for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < totalPages; pageNumber++) {
   209	                    if (shouldProcessPage(pageNumber, pagesToProcess)) {
   210	                        List<IObject> pageContents = HiddenTextProcessor.findHiddenText(
   211	                            inputPdfName, contents.get(pageNumber), true, config.getPassword());
   212	                        contents.set(pageNumber, pageContents);
   213	                    }
   214	                }
   215	            }
   216	
   217	            boolean structured = config.needsStructuredProcessing();
   218	
   219	            // ClusterTableProcessor: whole-document (must be sequential)
   220	            if (structured && config.isClusterTableMethod()) {
   221	                new ClusterTableProcessor().processTables(contents);
   222	            }
   223	
   224	            // Loop 2: TableBorder + TextLine per-page
   225	            pool.submit(() ->
   226	                IntStream.range(0, totalPages).parallel().forEach(pageNumber -> {
   227	                    if (!shouldProcessPage(pageNumber, pagesToProcess)) {
   228	                        return;
   229	                    }
   230	                    propagateState.run();
   231	                    List<IObject> pageContents = contents.get(pageNumber);
   232	                    if (structured) {
   233	                        pageContents = TableBorderProcessor.processTableBorders(pageContents, pageNumber);
   234	                        if (config.isDetectStrikethrough()) {
   235	                            StrikethroughProcessor.processStrikethroughs(pageContents);
   236	                        }
   237	                        pageContents = pageContents.stream().filter(x -> !(x instanceof LineChunk)).collect(Collectors.toList());
   238	                        pageContents = SpecialTableProcessor.detectSpecialTables(pageContents);
   239	                    }
   240	                    pageContents = TextLineProcessor.processTextLines(pageContents);
   241	                    contents.set(pageNumber, pageContents);
   242	                })
   243	            ).get();
   244	
   245	            if (structured) {
   246	                // Cross-page operations (must be sequential)
   247	                HeaderFooterProcessor.processHeadersAndFooters(contents, false);
   248	                ListProcessor.processLists(contents, false);
   249	            }
   250	
   251	            // Loop 3: Paragraph + Heading per-page (always need ParagraphProcessor for text output)
   252	            pool.submit(() ->
   253	                IntStream.range(0, totalPages).parallel().forEach(pageNumber -> {
   254	                    if (!shouldProcessPage(pageNumber, pagesToProcess)) {
   255	                        return;
   256	                    }
   257	                    propagateState.run();
   258	                    List<IObject> pageContents = contents.get(pageNumber);
   259	                    pageContents = ParagraphProcessor.processParagraphs(pageContents);
   260	                    if (structured) {
   261	                        pageContents = ListProcessor.processListsFromTextNodes(pageContents);
   262	                        HeadingProcessor.processHeadings(pageContents, false);
   263	                        CaptionProcessor.processCaptions(pageContents);
   264	                    }
   265	                    contents.set(pageNumber, pageContents);
   266	                })
   267	            ).get();
   268	
   269	            // Sequential ID assignment (must be in page order)
   270	            for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < totalPages; pageNumber++) {
   271	                if (shouldProcessPage(pageNumber, pagesToProcess)) {
   272	                    setIDs(contents.get(pageNumber));
   273	                }
   274	            }
   275	
   276	            if (structured) {
   277	                // Cross-page post-processing (must be sequential)
   278	                ListProcessor.checkNeighborLists(contents);
   279	                TableBorderProcessor.checkNeighborTables(contents);
   280	                HeadingProcessor.detectHeadingsLevels();
   281	                LevelProcessor.detectLevels(contents);
   282	            }
   283	        } catch (Exception e) {
   284	            throw new IOException("Parallel page processing failed", e);
   285	        } finally {
   286	            pool.shutdown();
   287	        }
   288	        return contents;
   289	    }
   290	
   291	    /**
   292	     * Checks if a page should be processed based on the filter.
   293	     *
   294	     * @param pageNumber 0-indexed page number
   295	     * @param pagesToProcess set of valid page numbers to process, or null for all pages
   296	     * @return true if the page should be processed
   297	     */
   298	    private static boolean shouldProcessPage(int pageNumber, Set<Integer> pagesToProcess) {
   299	        return pagesToProcess == null || pagesToProcess.contains(pageNumber);
   300	    }
   301	
   302	    private static void generateOutputs(String inputPdfName, List<List<IObject>> contents, Config config) throws IOException {
   303	        // Stdout mode: write primary format to stdout, skip file I/O
   304	        if (config.isOutputStdout()) {
   305	            java.io.Writer stdoutWriter = new java.io.BufferedWriter(
   306	                new java.io.OutputStreamWriter(System.out, java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   307	            if (config.isGenerateText()) {
   308	                TextGenerator textGenerator = new TextGenerator(stdoutWriter, config);

Now I need to understand the coordinate system. Looking at `DoclingSchemaTransformer.java:475`: `double rowHeight = (tableBbox.getTopY() - tableBbox.getBottomY()) / numRows;` — This suggests that `getTopY()` returns a larger value than `getBottomY()` (since height is positive). So `TopY` is the top of the bounding box (larger Y value) and `BottomY` is the bottom (smaller Y value). This is typical for PDF coordinate systems where Y increases upward.

So for a page with height H:
- `getTopY()` ≈ H (top of page)
- `getBottomY()` ≈ 0 (bottom of page)

Now let me re-examine `filterHeaderOrFooterContents`:

```java
private static List<IObject> filterHeaderOrFooterContents(List<IObject> contents, int pageNumber, boolean isHeaderDetection) {
    BoundingBox boundingBox = DocumentProcessor.getPageBoundingBox(pageNumber);
    if (boundingBox == null) {
        return contents;
    }
    List<IObject> result = new ArrayList<>();
    for (IObject content : contents) {
        if (isHeaderDetection) {
            if (content.getBottomY() < boundingBox.getHeight() * 2 / 3) {
                continue;
            }
        } else {
            if (content.getTopY() > boundingBox.getHeight() / 3) {
                continue;
            }
        }
        result.add(content);
    }
    return result;
}
```

For HEADERS (`isHeaderDetection=true`):
- SKIP (continue) if `content.getBottomY() < height * 2/3` → skips content whose bottom is below 2/3 of page height (i.e., in the bottom 2/3 of the page). Wait, `getBottomY()` is the lower Y coordinate. If content is at the top of the page, its `getBottomY()` would be close to `height`. For a header at the top, `bottomY` would be large (close to page height). If `bottomY < height * 2/3`, that means the content is in the bottom 2/3 of the page, so we skip it. This seems correct for headers: we keep content whose bottom is in the top 1/3.

For FOOTERS (`isHeaderDetection=false`):
- SKIP (continue) if `content.getTopY() > height / 3` → skips content whose top is above 1/3 of page height. This means we keep content whose top is in the bottom 2/3 of the page. 

But for footers, we should keep content near the BOTTOM of the page, not the bottom 2/3. The condition should be `content.getTopY() < height / 3` (keep content whose top is in the bottom 1/3) or equivalently, skip if `content.getTopY() > height / 3` is wrong — it should be skip if `content.getBottomY() > height / 3` (content extends into the top 2/3).

Wait, let me re-think. For footers:
- We want content near the bottom of the page.
- Bottom of page = Y close to 0.
- Top of page = Y close to height.
- So a footer would have `getTopY()` close to some small value (like 0 + footer_height) and `getBottomY()` close to 0.

For the footer check, we want to FILTER OUT content that is NOT near the bottom. Content that is too high up should be filtered out (skipped).

Current code: `if (content.getTopY() > boundingBox.getHeight() / 3) { continue; }` — This skips content whose top is ABOVE 1/3 of the page height. Wait, if `getTopY() > height/3`, that means the top of the content is in the top 2/3 of the page. This would skip content in the top 2/3 and KEEP content in the bottom 1/3. 

Actually wait: Y increases upward. So:
- `getTopY()` = large value = near top of page
- `getBottomY()` = small value = near bottom of page

If `getTopY() > height/3`, that means the top of the content is above the 1/3 line (i.e., in the top 2/3 of the page). So we skip it. This means we only keep content whose `getTopY() <= height/3`, i.e., content whose top is in the bottom 1/3 of the page.

That actually seems correct! But the problem is that the threshold `height/3` might be too generous for some documents. If the page height is e.g., 800, then `height/3 ≈ 267`. A footer at y=43 would have `getTopY() ≈ 43` which is well within the threshold. But a body note at y=116 would also have `getTopY() ≈ 116` which is also within the threshold (116 < 267). So the threshold is too large; it's allowing content in the bottom 1/3 of the page, which can be quite a lot of content.

The footer bbox is too large because it's absorbing body text that happens to be close to the actual footer. - Page 20: Footer bbox height 100.4 (abnormal), body note absorbed  
- Page 21: Footer bbox height 9.2 (normal)

This pattern suggests that on pages 19 and 20, there's a body note that appears at similar positions and gets matched as footer content. On page 21, the note doesn't appear, so the footer is correctly detected.

The key issue is: `arePossibleHeadersOrFooters` is matching body text across pages 19 and 20, treating it as footer content. The matching criteria in `arePossibleHeadersOrFooters`:
1. Bounding boxes must overlap (excluding page dimension)
2. Font sizes must be close
3. Either same text value OR matching interval pattern (like page numbers)

The body note "※ 출수 중 출수 버튼을 터치하면 출수가 정지됩니다." is identical on both pages, so it matches criterion 3 (same text value). And since it's near the bottom of the page, it gets included as a footer candidate.

But then `filterHeaderOrFooterContents` should filter it out if it's not near enough to the bottom. The threshold is `height/3`. If the page height is, say, 800, then `height/3 ≈ 267`. The body note at y=116 has `topY ≈ 116`, which is `< 267`, so it passes the filter (it's in the bottom 1/3 of the page).

The actual footer at y=43 is also in the bottom 1/3. The problem is the threshold `height/3` is too large — it should be something like `height * 0.15` or `height * 0.2` to only capture actual footers near the bottom edge.

But wait, let me also check: is the issue that the body text is included in the footer element, or that the footer bbox expands to include it? Looking at the PR: "Footer bounding box extends to y=135 (h≈100) instead of the normal y=43 (h≈9)." This means the footer's bounding box grows to encompass the body note, which is at y=116.

The footer element (`SemanticHeaderOrFooter`) contains multiple items, and its bounding box is the union of all its contents. If body text at y=116 is incorrectly included in the footer contents, the bbox expands.

So the fix should be to tighten the `filterHeaderOrFooterContents` method to be more restrictive about what can be considered a footer (or header). The threshold `height/3` (≈33% of page) is too generous. Footers are typically in the bottom 10-15% of a page.

But I also need to check if there's another issue: the `arePossibleHeadersOrFooters` function might also need to check vertical position. Let me look at it again:

```java
private static boolean arePossibleHeadersOrFooters(IObject object1, IObject object2, int increment) {
    if (object1 instanceof SemanticTextNode && object2 instanceof SemanticTextNode) {
        ...
        if (!BoundingBox.areOverlapsBoundingBoxesExcludingPages(...)) return false;
        if (!NodeUtils.areCloseNumbers(textNode1.getFontSize(), textNode2.getFontSize())) return false;
        if (Objects.equals(textNode1.getValue(), textNode2.getValue())) return true;
        ...
    }
    ...
}
```

It checks bounding box overlap (excluding page dimension), font size similarity, and text equality. But it doesn't check if the content is actually near the edge of the page. Body text in the middle of the page that happens to be identical across pages could be matched as header/footer.

The `filterHeaderOrFooterContents` is supposed to catch this, but its threshold is too loose.

Let me look at the tests to understand expected behavior better:

- Headers are near the top (Y close to page height)
- A header would have `bottomY` large (e.g., 750) and `topY` even larger (e.g., 800)
- Condition: `if (content.getBottomY() < boundingBox.getHeight() * 2 / 3) continue;`
  - `height * 2/3` = 800 * 2/3 ≈ 533
  - Header bottomY=750: 750 < 533? No → NOT skipped → kept ✓
  - But body text at middle with bottomY=400: 400 < 533? Yes → skipped ✓

So the header condition seems reasonably strict (keeps top 1/3), but the footer condition is too loose (keeps bottom 2/3? No wait...)

Let me re-examine: for footer, `continue` (skip) when `content.getTopY() > height/3`. This skips items whose top is above the 1/3 line. So it KEEPS items whose top is BELOW the 1/3 line, i.e., in the bottom 1/3. That's actually symmetric with the header condition.

But wait: the header condition skips when `content.getBottomY() < height * 2/3`. This skips items whose bottom is below the 2/3 line, i.e., KEEPS items whose bottom is above the 2/3 line (top 1/3).

So both are filtering to keep only the relevant 1/3 of the page. But 1/3 of a page can still be quite large. For a typical A4 page (height ~842 points), 1/3 is ~280 points, which is about 3.9 inches. A footer is typically much smaller than that.

The problem reported is that body text at y=116 gets absorbed. If the page height is, say, 842, then `height/3 = 280`. The body text at y=116 has `topY ≈ 116` which is `< 280`, so it's kept. But the actual footer at y=43 is also kept. Both are in the bottom 1/3.

The issue is that once items are identified as footer candidates by `getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage` (which checks for repeating patterns across pages), the `filterHeaderOrFooterContents` should be more restrictive to only keep items very close to the page edge.

Let me think about the right fix:

1. **Tighten the threshold**: Change `height/3` to something smaller like `height/4` or `height/5` or even a fixed value like 100 points.

2. **Add additional checks**: Maybe check that footer items are within a certain distance from the bottom edge, not just the top 1/3.

3. **Check the matching logic**: Maybe `arePossibleHeadersOrFooters` should also consider vertical position.

But actually, looking at the problem more holistically: the issue is that `getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage` identifies too many items as footer candidates because it matches body text that happens to repeat across pages. The `filterHeaderOrFooterContents` is supposed to filter out false positives but its threshold is too loose.

Let me also check if there's a concept of "how many items from the bottom" that goes wrong. The `getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage` counts how many consecutive items from the start/end match across pages. If body text on page 19 and 20 match (same note), and the actual footer also matches, then the count could be 2 (footer + body note) instead of 1 (just footer).

So the fix could be:
1. Make `filterHeaderOrFooterContents` more restrictive (smaller threshold).
2. Or add a check in `arePossibleHeadersOrFooters` or `getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage` to stop adding items once the position is too far from the edge.

Let me look at what changes have been made to similar issues in the codebase. Let me check if there are any recent fixes or related logic in other files.

   150	    private static List<Integer> getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage(List<List<IObject>> sortedContents, boolean isHeaderDetection) {
   151	        List<Integer> numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage = new ArrayList<>(sortedContents.size());
   152	        for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < sortedContents.size(); pageNumber++) {
   153	            numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage.add(0);
   154	        }
   155	        int currentIndex = 0;
   156	        while (true) {
   157	            List<IObject> contents = new ArrayList<>(sortedContents.size());
   158	            for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < sortedContents.size(); pageNumber++) {
   159	                if (numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage.get(pageNumber) != currentIndex) {
   160	                    contents.add(null);
   161	                    continue;
   162	                }
   163	                List<IObject> pageContents = sortedContents.get(pageNumber);
   164	                int index = isHeaderDetection ? currentIndex : pageContents.size() - 1 - currentIndex;
   165	                if (index >= 0 && index < pageContents.size()) {
   166	                    contents.add(pageContents.get(index));
   167	                } else {
   168	                    contents.add(null);
   169	                }
   170	            }
   171	            Set<Integer> newIndexes = getIndexesOfHeaderOrFootersContents(contents);
   172	            if (newIndexes.isEmpty()) {
   173	                break;
   174	            }
   175	            for (Integer newIndex : newIndexes) {
   176	                numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage.set(newIndex, currentIndex + 1);
   177	            }
   178	            currentIndex++;
   179	        }
   180	        return numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage;
   181	    }
   182	
   183	    private static Set<Integer> getIndexesOfHeaderOrFootersContents(List<IObject> contents) {
   184	        Set<Integer> result = new HashSet<>(contents.size());
   185	        for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < contents.size() - 1; pageNumber++) {
   186	            IObject currentObject = contents.get(pageNumber);
   187	            IObject nextObject = contents.get(pageNumber + 1);
   188	            if (currentObject != null && nextObject != null) {
   189	                if (arePossibleHeadersOrFooters(currentObject, nextObject, 1)) {
   190	                    result.add(pageNumber);
   191	                    result.add(pageNumber + 1);
   192	                }
   193	            }
   194	        }
   195	        //2-page style
   196	        for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < contents.size() - 2; pageNumber++) {
   197	            IObject currentObject = contents.get(pageNumber);
   198	            IObject nextObject = contents.get(pageNumber + 2);
   199	            if (currentObject != null && nextObject != null) {
   200	                if (arePossibleHeadersOrFooters(currentObject, nextObject, 2)) {
   201	                    result.add(pageNumber);
   202	                    result.add(pageNumber + 2);
   203	                }
   204	            }
   205	        }
   206	        return result;

   514	    public static List<IObject> sortPageContents(List<IObject> contents) {
   515	        if (contents == null || contents.isEmpty()) {
   516	            return contents;
   517	        }
   518	        List<IObject> sortedContents = new ArrayList<>(contents);
   519	        sortedContents.sort((o1, o2) -> {
   520	            BoundingBox b1 = o1.getBoundingBox();
   521	            BoundingBox b2 = o2.getBoundingBox();
   522	            if (b1 == null && b2 == null) {
   523	                return 0;
   524	            }
   525	            if (b1 == null) {
   526	                return 1;
   527	            }
   528	            if (b2 == null) {
   529	                return -1;
   530	            }

   532	                return b1.getPageNumber() - b2.getPageNumber();
   533	            }
   534	            if (!Objects.equals(b1.getLastPageNumber(), b2.getLastPageNumber())) {
   535	                return b1.getLastPageNumber() - b2.getLastPageNumber();
   536	            }
   537	            if (!Objects.equals(b1.getTopY(), b2.getTopY())) {
   538	                return b2.getTopY() - b1.getTopY() > 0 ? 1 : -1;
   539	            }
   540	            if (!Objects.equals(b1.getLeftX(), b2.getLeftX())) {
   541	                return b1.getLeftX() - b2.getLeftX() > 0 ? 1 : -1;

   547	                return b1.getRightX() - b2.getRightX() > 0 ? 1 : -1;
   548	            }
   549	            return 0;
   550	        });
   551	        return sortedContents;

So sorting is by `topY` descending (higher Y first = top of page first). So the first items are at the top of the page, and the last items are at the bottom of the page.

Now, for footers:
- It starts at index 0 from the bottom: `pageContents.size() - 1 - 0` = last item (lowest topY, bottom of page)
- If the last items on consecutive pages match, those pages get count=1
- Then it moves to index 1 from bottom: `pageContents.size() - 1 - 1` = second-to-last item
- If those match on the SAME pages that already had count=1, they get count=2
- Etc.

Now, let me think about the proper fix. Looking at the code again:

```java
private static List<IObject> filterHeaderOrFooterContents(List<IObject> contents, int pageNumber, boolean isHeaderDetection) {
    BoundingBox boundingBox = DocumentProcessor.getPageBoundingBox(pageNumber);
    if (boundingBox == null) {
        return contents;
    }
    List<IObject> result = new ArrayList<>();
    for (IObject content : contents) {
        if (isHeaderDetection) {
            if (content.getBottomY() < boundingBox.getHeight() * 2 / 3) {
                continue;
            }
        } else {
            if (content.getTopY() > boundingBox.getHeight() / 3) {
                continue;
            }
        }
        result.add(content);
    }
    return result;
}
```

The intention:
- For headers: keep items whose bottom is in the top 1/3 of the page
- For footers: keep items whose top is in the bottom 1/3 of the page

But 1/3 is too large. It should be more like 1/5 or 1/6.

However, I'm also concerned about the condition logic. Let me trace through an example:

Page height = 100 (for simplicity), Y from 0 (bottom) to 100 (top).

Footer at bottom: topY=10, bottomY=0.
- Footer check: `topY > height/3` → 10 > 33? No → keep. ✓

Body note at y=30: topY=40, bottomY=30.
- Footer check: `topY > height/3` → 40 > 33? Yes → skip. ✓ (Wait, this would be filtered out!)

But the PR says body note at y=116 gets absorbed. If page height is ~800, then height/3 ≈ 267. Body note topY ≈ 116: 116 > 267? No → keep. That's why it gets absorbed.

So the threshold `height/3` is too large. Changing it to `height/5` (800/5 = 160) would still keep the body note (116 < 160). Changing to `height/6` (800/6 ≈ 133) would still keep it (116 < 133). Changing to `height/7` (800/7 ≈ 114) would filter it out (116 > 114).

But we can't use a threshold that depends on the specific page height and note position. A better approach might be to use a fixed threshold (like 100 points from the bottom edge) or a percentage that's more appropriate for footers (like 15%).

Actually, looking at the problem from a different angle: the issue is that `getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage` greedily adds items as long as they match across pages. It should STOP adding items once the items are too far from the page edge. This could be done by adding a position check in the loop.

Let me look at the loop again:

```java
int currentIndex = 0;
while (true) {
    List<IObject> contents = new ArrayList<>(sortedContents.size());
    for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < sortedContents.size(); pageNumber++) {
        if (numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage.get(pageNumber) != currentIndex) {
            contents.add(null);
            continue;
        }
        List<IObject> pageContents = sortedContents.get(pageNumber);
        int index = isHeaderDetection ? currentIndex : pageContents.size() - 1 - currentIndex;
        if (index >= 0 && index < pageContents.size()) {
            contents.add(pageContents.get(index));
        } else {
            contents.add(null);
        }
    }
    Set<Integer> newIndexes = getIndexesOfHeaderOrFootersContents(contents);
    if (newIndexes.isEmpty()) {
        break;
    }
    for (Integer newIndex : newIndexes) {
        numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage.set(newIndex, currentIndex + 1);
    }
    currentIndex++;
}
```

The loop continues adding items as long as there are matching items at the current index. It doesn't check if those items are actually near the edge. So if there's a repeating body text near the bottom, it gets included.

One approach: modify `getIndexesOfHeaderOrFootersContents` or the loop to also check position. But the cleanest approach might be to add a position check in the matching function `arePossibleHeadersOrFooters` or in the filter function.

Actually, I think the best fix is to modify `filterHeaderOrFooterContents` to be more restrictive. But instead of just changing the threshold, we should also consider that headers/footers should be close to the page edge. Let me change the threshold from `height/3` to `height/5` (20%) for footers and from `height*2/3` to `height*4/5` (80%) for headers.

But wait, I should also consider: what if the body note is at y=50 and page height is 800? Then even `height/5 = 160` would still include it. The problem is fundamentally that the algorithm allows non-edge content to be included.

Maybe the fix should be in `getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage`: it should break out of the loop not only when there are no matching items, but also when the current item is too far from the edge.

Let me think about this more carefully by looking at what data the algorithm works with.

The sorted contents for a page are sorted by topY descending. For footers:
- Index 0 from bottom = last item = item with smallest topY (closest to bottom)
- Index 1 from bottom = second-to-last item = item with second smallest topY
- etc.

So the algorithm starts from the bottom and works upward. If it finds matching items, it continues. If not, it stops.

The problem: the body note is between the actual footer and the main body text. Since the body note matches across pages, the algorithm continues past it, including it as footer.

I think the best fix is to add a position check in the loop of `getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage`. When considering items at `currentIndex`, if those items are too far from the edge, the loop should break.

For footers: if the item at `currentIndex` from the bottom has `topY > height * FOOTER_THRESHOLD`, it's too far from the bottom edge, so break.
For headers: if the item at `currentIndex` from the top has `bottomY < height * HEADER_THRESHOLD`, it's too far from the top edge, so break.

But this requires access to page dimensions. The page bounding box is available via `DocumentProcessor.getPageBoundingBox`.

Alternatively, I could modify `filterHeaderOrFooterContents` to not just filter individual items, but to truncate the list at the point where items are too far from the edge. But `filterHeaderOrFooterContents` receives the list of candidates and filters them; it could also stop at the first non-conforming item.

Wait, actually `filterHeaderOrFooterContents` receives a sublist that's already contiguous from the edge. For footers, it receives `pageContents.subList(pageContents.size() - currentIndex, pageContents.size())` which is the last `currentIndex` items. These are the items that were matched as footer candidates. If `filterHeaderOrFooterContents` filters out some items from the middle, it could break the contiguity.

But the real issue is that `currentIndex` is too large because it includes non-footer items. If we fix the loop to stop earlier, `currentIndex` would be correct and `filterHeaderOrFooterContents` might not even be needed (or its threshold could remain as a safety check).

Let me implement a fix in `getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage`. I'll add a position check that breaks the loop when items are too far from the edge.

Let me look at the method again:

```java
private static List<IObject> filterHeaderOrFooterContents(List<IObject> contents, int pageNumber, boolean isHeaderDetection) {
    BoundingBox boundingBox = DocumentProcessor.getPageBoundingBox(pageNumber);
    if (boundingBox == null) {
        return contents;
    }
    List<IObject> result = new ArrayList<>();
    for (IObject content : contents) {
        if (isHeaderDetection) {
            if (content.getBottomY() < boundingBox.getHeight() * 2 / 3) {
                continue;
            }
        } else {
            if (content.getTopY() > boundingBox.getHeight() / 3) {
                continue;
            }
        }
        result.add(content);
    }
    return result;
}
```

The contents are in order from the edge outward. For footers, the first item is the one closest to the bottom edge, then the next one, etc. If I encounter an item that's too far from the edge, I should break (stop adding more items) rather than just skipping it and continuing. This ensures that only a contiguous block from the edge is included.

Now, let me think more carefully about the right fix. I need to understand the coordinate system better.

Let me check the test's bounding boxes:
- Header: `new BoundingBox(0, 10.0, 30.0, 20.0, 40.0)` — page=0, leftX=10, bottomY=30, rightX=20, topY=40
- Text: `new BoundingBox(0, 10.0, 20.0, 20.0, 30.0)` — page=0, leftX=10, bottomY=20, rightX=20, topY=30
- Footer: `new BoundingBox(0, 10.0, 10.0, 20.0, 20.0)` — page=0, leftX=10, bottomY=10, rightX=20, topY=20

So topY > bottomY, Y increases upward. The page would have height from bottomY=0 to topY=40 (if these were the full page). Header is at top (30-40), footer at bottom (10-20).

Now for the PR issue:
- Normal footer: "y=43 (h≈9)" — This probably means the footer's topY≈43 and height≈9, so bottomY≈34.
- Body note: "y=116" — This is probably the topY of the body note.
- Page height: unknown, but if it's A4, crop box is typically [0, 0, 595.28, 841.89] (width x height), so height ≈ 842.

So:
- Footer: topY≈43, bottomY≈34
- Body note: topY≈116
- `height/3 ≈ 280` → footer (43 < 280) passes, body note (116 < 280) also passes
- `height/5 ≈ 168` → footer (43 < 168) passes, body note (116 < 168) also passes
- `height/6 ≈ 140` → footer (43 < 140) passes, body note (116 < 140) also passes
- `height/7 ≈ 120` → footer (43 < 120) passes, body note (116 < 120) also passes
- `height/8 ≈ 105` → footer (43 < 105) passes, body note (116 > 105) FILTERED OUT ✓

So I need `height/8` to filter out the body note. But `height/8` is 12.5% of page height, which might be too aggressive for some documents with larger footers.

However, I think there's another approach: instead of just changing the threshold, I should also modify the algorithm to check that the footer items are contiguous from the edge. The `getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage` could stop adding items when they're too far from the edge.

But actually, the more I think about it, the more I think the right fix is in `getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage`: it should incorporate a position check. Let me modify that method to break out of the while loop when the current item is too far from the page edge.

Let me check what page bounding box information is available in that method context.

Actually, I can get the page bounding box via `DocumentProcessor.getPageBoundingBox(pageNumber)` inside the loop. But I need to be careful about performance.

Let me implement a more comprehensive fix:

1. In `getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage`, add a check: before incrementing the count for a page, verify that the item is within a reasonable distance from the edge. If none of the matching items are close enough to the edge, break the loop.

2. Keep `filterHeaderOrFooterContents` as a second line of defense, with a more restrictive threshold.

Actually, let me reconsider the whole approach. The problem is really in `arePossibleHeadersOrFooters` or in the counting logic. The body note matches because it has identical text on both pages. But the algorithm should recognize that it's not a footer because it's too far from the edge.

The simplest and most effective fix would be to add a position check in `getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage`. When considering items at `currentIndex`, if for ALL pages that matched, the items are too far from the edge, then break. Or better: if for ANY matched page, the item is too far from the edge, don't count it (but still allow other pages that are close to the edge to be counted).

Wait, the algorithm works by: for each index from the edge, check if items across pages match. If pages 19 and 20 match at index 1 (body note), they get count incremented. But page 21 doesn't match (no body note), so it doesn't get incremented. The result is that pages 19-20 have count=2, page 21 has count=1.

The fix should prevent the body note from being counted even if it matches. I need to add a position check: an item is only eligible to be a header/footer if it's close enough to the page edge.

    39	/**
    40	 * Processor for detecting and extracting headers and footers from PDF documents.
    41	 * Identifies repeating content at the top and bottom of pages.
    42	 */
    43	public class HeaderFooterProcessor {
    44	
    45	    /**
    46	     * Processes document contents to detect headers and footers.
    47	     *
    48	     * @param contents the document contents organized by page
    49	     * @param isTagged whether the document is tagged
    50	     */
    51	    public static void processHeadersAndFooters(List<List<IObject>> contents, boolean isTagged) {
    52	        DocumentProcessor.setIndexesForDocumentContents(contents);
    53	        List<List<IObject>> sortedContents = new ArrayList<>();
    54	        for (List<IObject> content : contents) {
    55	            sortedContents.add(DocumentProcessor.sortPageContents(content));
    56	        }
    57	        List<List<IObject>> filteredSortedContents = new ArrayList<>();
    58	        for (List<IObject> content : sortedContents) {
    59	            filteredSortedContents.add(content.stream().filter(c -> !(c instanceof LineChunk) && !(c instanceof LineArtChunk)).collect(Collectors.toList()));
    60	        }
    61	        List<SemanticHeaderOrFooter> footers = getHeadersOrFooters(filteredSortedContents, false);
    62	        List<SemanticHeaderOrFooter> headers = getHeadersOrFooters(filteredSortedContents, true);
    63	        for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < contents.size(); pageNumber++) {
    64	            contents.set(pageNumber, updatePageContents(contents.get(pageNumber), headers.get(pageNumber), footers.get(pageNumber)));
    65	        }
    66	        if (!isTagged) {
    67	            processHeadersOrFootersContents(footers);
    68	            processHeadersOrFootersContents(headers);
    69	        }
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    private static void processHeadersOrFootersContents(List<SemanticHeaderOrFooter> headersOrFooters) {
    73	        for (SemanticHeaderOrFooter headerOrFooter : headersOrFooters) {
    74	            if (headerOrFooter != null) {
    75	                headerOrFooter.setContents(processHeaderOrFooterContent(headerOrFooter.getContents()));
    76	            }
    77	        }
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    private static List<IObject> updatePageContents(List<IObject> pageContents, SemanticHeaderOrFooter header, SemanticHeaderOrFooter footer) {
    81	        SortedSet<Integer> headerAndFooterIndexes = new TreeSet<>();
    82	        headerAndFooterIndexes.addAll(getHeaderOrFooterContentsIndexes(header));
    83	        headerAndFooterIndexes.addAll(getHeaderOrFooterContentsIndexes(footer));
    84	        if (headerAndFooterIndexes.isEmpty()) {
    85	            return pageContents;
    86	        }
    87	        List<IObject> result = new ArrayList<>();
    88	        if (header != null) {
    89	            result.add(header);
    90	        }
    91	        Iterator<Integer> iterator = headerAndFooterIndexes.iterator();
    92	        int nextHeaderOrFooterIndex = iterator.hasNext() ? iterator.next() : pageContents.size();
    93	        for (int index = 0; index < pageContents.size(); index++) {
    94	            if (index < nextHeaderOrFooterIndex) {
    95	                result.add(pageContents.get(index));
    96	            } else {
    97	                nextHeaderOrFooterIndex = iterator.hasNext() ? iterator.next() : pageContents.size();
    98	            }
    99	        }
   100	        if (footer != null) {
   101	            result.add(footer);
   102	        }
   103	        return result;
   104	    }
   105	
   106	    private static Set<Integer> getHeaderOrFooterContentsIndexes(SemanticHeaderOrFooter header) {
   107	        if (header == null) {
   108	            return Collections.emptySet();
   109	        }
   110	        SortedSet<Integer> set = new TreeSet<>();
   111	        for (IObject content : header.getContents()) {
   112	            set.add(content.getIndex());
   113	        }
   114	        return set;
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    private static List<SemanticHeaderOrFooter> getHeadersOrFooters(List<List<IObject>> sortedContents, boolean isHeaderDetection) {
   118	        List<SemanticHeaderOrFooter> headersOrFooters = new ArrayList<>(sortedContents.size());
   119	        List<Integer> numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage = getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage(sortedContents, isHeaderDetection);
   120	        for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < sortedContents.size(); pageNumber++) {
   121	            Integer currentIndex = numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage.get(pageNumber);
   122	            if (currentIndex == 0) {
   123	                headersOrFooters.add(null);
   124	                continue;
   125	            }
   126	            List<IObject> pageContents = sortedContents.get(pageNumber);
   127	            List<IObject> headerContents = filterHeaderOrFooterContents(isHeaderDetection ? pageContents.subList(0, currentIndex) :
   128	                    pageContents.subList(pageContents.size() - currentIndex, pageContents.size()), pageNumber, isHeaderDetection);
   129	            if (headerContents.isEmpty()) {
   130	                headersOrFooters.add(null);
   131	                continue;
   132	            }
   133	            SemanticHeaderOrFooter semanticHeaderOrFooter = new SemanticHeaderOrFooter(isHeaderDetection ? SemanticType.HEADER : SemanticType.FOOTER);
   134	            semanticHeaderOrFooter.addContents(headerContents);
   135	            semanticHeaderOrFooter.setRecognizedStructureId(StaticLayoutContainers.incrementContentId());
   136	            headersOrFooters.add(semanticHeaderOrFooter);
   137	        }
   138	        return headersOrFooters;
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    private static List<IObject> processHeaderOrFooterContent(List<IObject> contents) {
   142	        List<IObject> newContents = ParagraphProcessor.processParagraphs(contents);
   143	        newContents = ListProcessor.processListsFromTextNodes(newContents);
   144	        HeadingProcessor.processHeadings(newContents, false);
   145	        DocumentProcessor.setIDs(newContents);
   146	        CaptionProcessor.processCaptions(newContents);
   147	        return newContents;
   148	    }
   149	
   150	    private static List<Integer> getNumberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage(List<List<IObject>> sortedContents, boolean isHeaderDetection) {
   151	        List<Integer> numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage = new ArrayList<>(sortedContents.size());
   152	        for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < sortedContents.size(); pageNumber++) {
   153	            numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage.add(0);
   154	        }
   155	        int currentIndex = 0;
   156	        while (true) {
   157	            List<IObject> contents = new ArrayList<>(sortedContents.size());
   158	            for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < sortedContents.size(); pageNumber++) {
   159	                if (numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage.get(pageNumber) != currentIndex) {
   160	                    contents.add(null);
   161	                    continue;
   162	                }
   163	                List<IObject> pageContents = sortedContents.get(pageNumber);
   164	                int index = isHeaderDetection ? currentIndex : pageContents.size() - 1 - currentIndex;
   165	                if (index >= 0 && index < pageContents.size()) {
   166	                    contents.add(pageContents.get(index));
   167	                } else {
   168	                    contents.add(null);
   169	                }
   170	            }
   171	            Set<Integer> newIndexes = getIndexesOfHeaderOrFootersContents(contents);
   172	            if (newIndexes.isEmpty()) {
   173	                break;
   174	            }
   175	            // Filter out pages where the current item is too far from the page edge
   176	            Set<Integer> validIndexes = new HashSet<>();
   177	            for (Integer newIndex : newIndexes) {
   178	                IObject content = contents.get(newIndex);
   179	                BoundingBox pageBoundingBox = DocumentProcessor.getPageBoundingBox(newIndex);
   180	                if (pageBoundingBox != null && content != null) {
   181	                    if (isHeaderDetection) {
   182	                        // Header items should be near the top of the page
   183	                        if (content.getBottomY() >= pageBoundingBox.getHeight() * 4 / 5) {
   184	                            validIndexes.add(newIndex);
   185	                        }
   186	                    } else {
   187	                        // Footer items should be near the bottom of the page
   188	                        if (content.getTopY() <= pageBoundingBox.getHeight() / 5) {
   189	                            validIndexes.add(newIndex);
   190	                        }
   191	                    }
   192	                } else if (pageBoundingBox == null) {
   193	                    // If we can't get the page bounding box, allow the item
   194	                    validIndexes.add(newIndex);
   195	                }
   196	            }
   197	            if (validIndexes.isEmpty()) {
   198	                break;
   199	            }
   200	            for (Integer newIndex : validIndexes) {
   201	                numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage.set(newIndex, currentIndex + 1);
   202	            }
   203	            currentIndex++;
   204	        }
   205	        return numberOfHeaderOrFooterContentsForEachPage;
   206	    }
   207	
   208	    private static Set<Integer> getIndexesOfHeaderOrFootersContents(List<IObject> contents) {
   209	        Set<Integer> result = new HashSet<>(contents.size());
   210	        for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < contents.size() - 1; pageNumber++) {
   211	            IObject currentObject = contents.get(pageNumber);
   212	            IObject nextObject = contents.get(pageNumber + 1);
   213	            if (currentObject != null && nextObject != null) {
   214	                if (arePossibleHeadersOrFooters(currentObject, nextObject, 1)) {
   215	                    result.add(pageNumber);
   216	                    result.add(pageNumber + 1);
   217	                }
   218	            }
   219	        }
   220	        //2-page style
   221	        for (int pageNumber = 0; pageNumber < contents.size() - 2; pageNumber++) {
   222	            IObject currentObject = contents.get(pageNumber);
   223	            IObject nextObject = contents.get(pageNumber + 2);
   224	            if (currentObject != null && nextObject != null) {
   225	                if (arePossibleHeadersOrFooters(currentObject, nextObject, 2)) {
   226	                    result.add(pageNumber);
   227	                    result.add(pageNumber + 2);
   228	                }
   229	            }
   230	        }
   231	        return result;
   232	    }
   233	
   234	    /**
   235	     * Checks if a content object is a header or footer.
   236	     *
   237	     * @param content the content object to check
   238	     * @return true if the content is a header or footer, false otherwise
   239	     */
   240	    public static boolean isHeaderOrFooter(IObject content) {
   241	        if (content instanceof INode) {
   242	            INode node = (INode) content;
   243	            if (node.getSemanticType() == SemanticType.HEADER || node.getSemanticType() == SemanticType.FOOTER) {
   244	                return true;
   245	            }
   246	        }
   247	        return false;
   248	    }
   249	
   250	    private static List<IObject> filterHeaderOrFooterContents(List<IObject> contents, int pageNumber, boolean isHeaderDetection) {
   251	        BoundingBox boundingBox = DocumentProcessor.getPageBoundingBox(pageNumber);
   252	        if (boundingBox == null) {
   253	            return contents;
   254	        }
   255	        List<IObject> result = new ArrayList<>();
   256	        for (IObject content : contents) {
   257	            if (isHeaderDetection) {
   258	                if (content.getBottomY() < boundingBox.getHeight() * 4 / 5) {
   259	                    continue;
   260	                }
   261	            } else {
   262	                if (content.getTopY() > boundingBox.getHeight() / 5) {
   263	                    continue;
   264	                }
   265	            }
   266	            result.add(content);
   267	        }
   268	        return result;
   269	    }
   270	
   271	    private static boolean arePossibleHeadersOrFooters(IObject object1, IObject object2, int increment) {
   272	        if (object1 instanceof SemanticTextNode && object2 instanceof SemanticTextNode) {
   273	            SemanticTextNode textNode1 = (SemanticTextNode) object1;
   274	            SemanticTextNode textNode2 = (SemanticTextNode) object2;
   275	            if (!BoundingBox.areOverlapsBoundingBoxesExcludingPages(object1.getBoundingBox(), object2.getBoundingBox())) {
   276	                return false;
   277	            }
   278	            if (!NodeUtils.areCloseNumbers(textNode1.getFontSize(), textNode2.getFontSize())) {
   279	                return false;
   280	            }
   281	            if (Objects.equals(textNode1.getValue(), textNode2.getValue())) {
   282	                return true;
   283	            }
   284	            List<SemanticTextNode> textNodes = new ArrayList<>(2);
   285	            textNodes.add(textNode1);
   286	            textNodes.add(textNode2);
   287	            if (getHeadersOrFootersIntervals(textNodes, increment).size() == 1) {
   288	                return true;
   289	            }
   290	        } else if (object1 instanceof TextLine && object2 instanceof TextLine) {
   291	            TextLine line1 = (TextLine) object1;
   292	            TextLine line2 = (TextLine) object2;
   293	            SemanticTextNode textNode1 = new SemanticTextNode();
   294	            textNode1.add(line1);
   295	            SemanticTextNode textNode2 = new SemanticTextNode();
   296	            textNode2.add(line2);
   297	            return arePossibleHeadersOrFooters(textNode1, textNode2, increment);
   298	        } else {
   299	            if (BoundingBox.areSameBoundingBoxesExcludingPages(object1.getBoundingBox(), object2.getBoundingBox())) {
   300	                return true;
   301	            }
   302	        }
   303	        return false;
   304	    }
   305	
   306	    private static Set<ListInterval> getHeadersOrFootersIntervals(List<SemanticTextNode> textNodes, int increment) {
   307	        List<ListItemTextInfo> textChildrenInfo = new ArrayList<>(textNodes.size());
   308	        for (int i = 0; i < textNodes.size(); i++) {
   309	            SemanticTextNode textNode = textNodes.get(i);
   310	            TextLine line = textNode.getFirstNonSpaceLine();
   311	            TextLine secondLine = textNode.getNonSpaceLine(1);
   312	            textChildrenInfo.add(new ListItemTextInfo(i, textNode.getSemanticType(),
   313	                    line, line.getValue().trim(), secondLine == null));
   314	        }
   315	        Set<ListInterval> intervals = getHeadersOfFooterIntervals(textChildrenInfo, increment);
   316	        return intervals;
   317	    }
   318	
   319	    private static Set<ListInterval> getHeadersOfFooterIntervals(List<ListItemTextInfo> itemsInfo, int increment) {

   321	        listIntervals.putAll((new AlfaLettersListLabelsDetectionAlgorithm1(increment)).getItemsIntervals(itemsInfo));

   323	        listIntervals.putAll((new KoreanLettersListLabelsDetectionAlgorithm(increment)).getItemsIntervals(itemsInfo));
   324	        listIntervals.putAll((new RomanNumbersListLabelsDetectionAlgorithm(increment)).getItemsIntervals(itemsInfo));

        BoundingBox boundingBox = DocumentProcessor.getPageBoundingBox(pageNumber);
        if (boundingBox == null) {
            return contents;
        }
        List<IObject> result = new ArrayList<>();
        if (isHeaderDetection) {
            // Headers: iterate from top edge outward (first items are closest to top)
            for (IObject content : contents) {
                if (content.getBottomY() < boundingBox.getHeight() * 4 / 5) {
                    break;
                }
                result.add(content);
            }
        } else {
            // Footers: iterate from bottom edge outward (last items are closest to bottom)
            for (int i = contents.size() - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                IObject content = contents.get(i);
                if (content.getTopY() > boundingBox.getHeight() / 5) {
                    break;
                }
                result.add(content);
            }
            // Restore original order (closest to edge first)
            Collections.reverse(result);
        }
        return result;
    }'

        if (boundingBox == null) {

        BoundingBox boundingBox = DocumentProcessor.getPageBoundingBox(pageNumber);
        if (boundingBox == null) {
            return contents;
        }
        List<IObject> result = new ArrayList<>();
        if (isHeaderDetection) {
            // Headers: iterate from top edge outward (first items are closest to top)
            for (IObject content : contents) {
                if (content.getBottomY() < boundingBox.getHeight() * 5 / 6) {
                    break;
                }
                result.add(content);
            }
        } else {
            // Footers: iterate from bottom edge outward (last items are closest to bottom)
            for (int i = contents.size() - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                IObject content = contents.get(i);
                if (content.getTopY() > boundingBox.getHeight() / 6) {
                    break;
                }
                result.add(content);
            }
            // Restore original order (closest to edge first)
            Collections.reverse(result);
        }
        return result;
